\index{\+\_\+pygame.\+h@{\+\_\+pygame.\+h}!P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE@{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}}
\index{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE@{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}!\+\_\+pygame.\+h@{\+\_\+pygame.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE}{PG\_HAVE\_CAPSULE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+S\+U\+LE~0}

This header file includes all the definitions for the base pygame extensions. This header only requires S\+DL and Python includes. The reason for functions prototyped with \#define\textquotesingle{}s is to allow for maximum python portability. It also uses python as the runtime linker, which allows for late binding. For more information on this style of development, read the Python docs on this subject. \href{http://www.python.org/doc/current/ext/using-cobjects.html}{\tt http\+://www.\+python.\+org/doc/current/ext/using-\/cobjects.\+html}

If using this to build your own derived extensions, you\textquotesingle{}ll see that the functions available here are mainly used to help convert between python objects and S\+DL objects. Since this library doesn\textquotesingle{}t add a lot of functionality to the S\+DL libarary, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to offer a lot either.

When initializing your extension module, you must manually import the modules you want to use. (this is the part about using python as the runtime linker). Each module has its own import\+\_\+xxx() routine. You need to perform this import after you have initialized your own module, and before you call any routines from that module. Since every module in pygame does this, there are plenty of examples.

The base module does include some useful conversion routines that you are free to use in your own extension.

When making changes, it is very important to keep the F\+I\+R\+S\+T\+S\+L\+OT and N\+U\+M\+S\+L\+OT constants up to date for each section. Also be sure not to overlap any of the slots. When you do make a mistake with this, it will result is a dereferenced N\+U\+LL pointer that is easier to diagnose than it could be \+:\mbox{]} \mbox{\Hypertarget{__pygame_8h_a9770ad8201237baffef5b9ee5908409d}\label{__pygame_8h_a9770ad8201237baffef5b9ee5908409d}} 
\index{\+\_\+pygame.\+h@{\+\_\+pygame.\+h}!P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT@{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT}}
\index{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT@{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT}!\+\_\+pygame.\+h@{\+\_\+pygame.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT}{PG\_HAVE\_COBJECT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define P\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+B\+J\+E\+CT~0}
